    <script>
     jQuery(function() {
	LGI.overlay.init(document.getElementById('lgi-overlay-depricated_browser'));
});

$(document).ready(function () {

    function setOverlay() {

        var e = $("#lgi-overlay-depricated_browser");

        var height = e.height();//parseInt(e.css("height"));
        var width = e.width();//parseInt(e.css("width"));

        var savedHeight = 400;
        var savedWidth = 700;

        var screenHeight = $(window).height();
        var screenWidth = $(window).width();

        if (screenHeight >= savedHeight) {
            e.css({"position": "fixed"});
        } else {
            e.css({"position": "absolute"});
        }
        if (screenWidth < savedWidth) {
            e.css({"width": screenWidth - 15 + "px"});
        } else {
            e.css({"width": savedWidth + "px"});
        }

        // center the modal
        var top = ((screenHeight / 2) - (height / 2) < 0) ? 0 : (screenHeight / 2) - (height / 2);
        var left = ((screenWidth / 2) - (width / 2) < 0) ? 0 : (screenWidth / 2) - (width / 2);

        e.css({
            "left": left + "px",
            "top": top + "px"
        });
    }

    $(window).bind('resize', function () {
        setOverlay();

    });
    $(window).bind('orientationchange', function () {
        setOverlay();
    });

    /*delayed execution to let the modal script set it's values first. This prevents
     * conflicts */
    setTimeout(function () {
        setOverlay();
    }, 100);

});
    </script>
   </div>
  </div>

        window.UPC = window.UPC || {};
        window.UPC.vars = window.UPC.vars || {};

        var siteCatalystPropertyString = '{}';
        var siteCatalystJsonObject = JSON.parse(siteCatalystPropertyString);

        for (var property in siteCatalystJsonObject) {
            if (siteCatalystJsonObject.hasOwnProperty(property)) {
                window.UPC.vars[property] = siteCatalystJsonObject[property];
            }
        }
    })();

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function animateTiles() {
    if($(window).width() > 768){
        setTimeout(function () {
            $('.intent-tiles').addClass('stagger');
        },250);
        setTimeout(function () {
            $('.intent-tiles-wrapper').addClass('doneLoading');
        }, 1100);
    }
    else{
        setTimeout(function () {
            $('.intent-tiles-wrapper').addClass('doneLoading');
        }, 150);
        setTimeout(function () {
            $('.intent-tiles').addClass('mobStagger');
        }, 900);
    }
}

$(document).ready(function () {
    animateTiles();

    $(window).on('resize', function () {
        animateTiles();
    });

});
